function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.501!');

	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_country_access');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_country_access');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_country_access')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_country_access', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}

}

	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_10();
if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql');
} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql') != 'a2c76e6fd6c4795bf0d71f3a381991b556b02598') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql');
}

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql') !== '9ec3eebfb93c8b0b1362ec89ee99d881f2f4f8bc') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql') != '5d2486d9677f40a776504745e7e56bd910f057b3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql') !== '5d2486d9677f40a776504745e7e56bd910f057b3') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql') !== '07008bd6b30da2d173a4832d92b8c8f64c985c77') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql') !== '5d2486d9677f40a776504745e7e56bd910f057b3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite') != 'a06473c8d8dcdf18581a6b1c7b1367fb261fbbbf') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite') !== 'a06473c8d8dcdf18581a6b1c7b1367fb261fbbbf') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite') !== '940e99600857e41d5c057ff7164386d77907f165') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite') !== 'a06473c8d8dcdf18581a6b1c7b1367fb261fbbbf') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/test_database_plugins')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/test_database_plugins');
	writefile_16();
	if (!is_file('dev/test_database_plugins')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/test_database_plugins');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') != '985c82c545d6d96905251b83c94550a998546f00') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/test_database_plugins');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/test_database_plugins', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/test_database_plugins');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') !== '985c82c545d6d96905251b83c94550a998546f00') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') !== '94a2f165700c7fe4113cdc58813c489c0616406c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/test_database_plugins');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/test_database_plugins');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/test_database_plugins')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/test_database_plugins', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_16();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') !== '985c82c545d6d96905251b83c94550a998546f00') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/test_database_plugins');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != 'b7c23d0580804829dc0cf389045e48ed5e2a471d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'b7c23d0580804829dc0cf389045e48ed5e2a471d') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'b6c0f6af9c7faf1222f2a7ec3de4353243f109cd') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'b7c23d0580804829dc0cf389045e48ed5e2a471d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_20();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php') != '09312c45ceb3e05c5c6bd858f7099967d0f991ab') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php', 0644)) {

	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php') !== '09312c45ceb3e05c5c6bd858f7099967d0f991ab') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php') !== 'ed76213c68e1511ba642f95cf0e07e7c8b5f4690') {

			if (!@copy('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php') !== '09312c45ceb3e05c5c6bd858f7099967d0f991ab') {

if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/index.php');
	writefile_34();
	if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/index.php') != 'e6dd4547171ef1473d7dd4e8ba73d863b1012bd2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'e6dd4547171ef1473d7dd4e8ba73d863b1012bd2') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '8188bf3a48ff08dde7d70b234f38b4c1c907088b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_34();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'e6dd4547171ef1473d7dd4e8ba73d863b1012bd2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	writefile_35();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') != 'c33759083e72114ad584f943ea4b1ca0253a118a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== 'c33759083e72114ad584f943ea4b1ca0253a118a') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== '6d79fdb6d2af69a7ef1e69fb2cbc8cb30840ff34') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_35();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== 'c33759083e72114ad584f943ea4b1ca0253a118a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 502\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 502') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3
